DOCKERFILE:
  # Use platform flag to enforce x86_64 architecture
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/opt/sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=$SDKMAN_DIR/candidates/java/current
  # Install base system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      sudo \
      unzip \
      zip \
      ca-certificates \
      bzip2 \
      libgl1-mesa-glx \
      libgtk-3-0 \
      libdbus-glib-1-2 \
      libxt6 \
      libx11-xcb1 \
      libxcomposite1 \
      libxcursor1 \
      libxdamage1 \
      libxext6 \
      libxfixes3 \
      libxi6 \
      libxrandr2 \
      libxrender1 \
      libxss1 \
      libxtst6 \
      libnss3 \
      libasound2 \
      libpangocairo-1.0-0 \
      libpango-1.0-0 \
      libatk1.0-0 \
      libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
      default-jre-headless \
      maven \
      firefox \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install GeckoDriver v0.31.0 for x86_64 Linux
  RUN GECKODRIVER_VERSION=v0.31.0 && \
      curl -L -o /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz https://github.com/mozilla/geckodriver/releases/download/$GECKODRIVER_VERSION/geckodriver-$GECKODRIVER_VERSION-linux64.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz -C /usr/local/bin/ && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/geckodriver && \
      rm /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz
  # Install Miniconda for Linux x86_64
  RUN MINICONDA_VERSION=py39_23.3.1-1 && \
      curl -L -o /tmp/miniconda.sh https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-$MINICONDA_VERSION-Linux-x86_64.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      $CONDA_DIR/bin/conda clean -tipsy && \
      ln -s $CONDA_DIR/etc/profile.d/conda.sh /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  # Create user itdocker with sudo privileges
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash itdocker && echo "itdocker ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" > /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker && chmod 0440 /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker
  # Install SDKMAN for Java management and install Java 8.0.302-open
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk install java 8.0.302-open && sdk default java 8.0.302-open"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/home/itdocker/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/home/itdocker/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  USER root
  # Set workdir to itdocker home
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  # Clone exli and inlinetest repositories
  RUN git clone https://github.com/se-sic/exli.git && \
      git clone https://github.com/se-sic/inlinetest.git
  # Copy prepare-conda-env.sh into container and make it executable
  COPY python/prepare-conda-env.sh /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  RUN chmod +x /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  # Run prepare-conda-env.sh to create conda env and install dependencies
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && bash /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh"
  # Install exli python package inside conda environment
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate exli && pip install /home/itdocker/exli/python"
  # Setup directory structure and permissions for logs, results, tests
  RUN mkdir -p /home/itdocker/exli/logs /home/itdocker/exli/results /home/itdocker/exli/tests && \
      chown -R itdocker:itdocker /home/itdocker/exli
  # Set user to itdocker and default working directory
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli
  # Start bash shell by default
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  # Use platform flag to enforce x86_64 architecture
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/opt/sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=$SDKMAN_DIR/candidates/java/current
  # Install base system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      sudo \
      unzip \
      zip \
      ca-certificates \
      bzip2 \
      libgl1-mesa-glx \
      libgtk-3-0 \
      libdbus-glib-1-2 \
      libxt6 \
      libx11-xcb1 \
      libxcomposite1 \
      libxcursor1 \
      libxdamage1 \
      libxext6 \
      libxfixes3 \
      libxi6 \
      libxrandr2 \
      libxrender1 \
      libxss1 \
      libxtst6 \
      libnss3 \
      libasound2 \
      libpangocairo-1.0-0 \
      libpango-1.0-0 \
      libatk1.0-0 \
      libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
      default-jre-headless \
      maven \
      firefox \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install GeckoDriver v0.31.0 for x86_64 Linux
  RUN GECKODRIVER_VERSION=v0.31.0 && \
      curl -L -o /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz https://github.com/mozilla/geckodriver/releases/download/$GECKODRIVER_VERSION/geckodriver-$GECKODRIVER_VERSION-linux64.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz -C /usr/local/bin/ && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/geckodriver && \
      rm /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz
  # Install Miniconda for Linux x86_64
  RUN MINICONDA_VERSION=py39_23.3.1-1 && \
      curl -L -o /tmp/miniconda.sh https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-$MINICONDA_VERSION-Linux-x86_64.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -tipsy && \
      ln -s /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  # Create user itdocker with sudo privileges
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash itdocker && echo "itdocker ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" > /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker && chmod 0440 /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker
  # Install SDKMAN for Java management and install Java 8.0.302-open
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk install java 8.0.302-open && sdk default java 8.0.302-open"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/home/itdocker/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/home/itdocker/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  USER root
  # Set workdir to itdocker home
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  # Clone exli and inlinetest repositories
  RUN git clone https://github.com/se-sic/exli.git && \
      git clone https://github.com/se-sic/inlinetest.git
  # Copy prepare-conda-env.sh into container and make it executable
  COPY python/prepare-conda-env.sh /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  RUN chmod +x /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  # Run prepare-conda-env.sh to create conda env and install dependencies
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && bash /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh"
  # Install exli python package inside conda environment
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate exli && pip install /home/itdocker/exli/python"
  # Setup directory structure and permissions for logs, results, tests
  RUN mkdir -p /home/itdocker/exli/logs /home/itdocker/exli/results /home/itdocker/exli/tests && \
      chown -R itdocker:itdocker /home/itdocker/exli
  # Set user to itdocker and default working directory at repo root
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli
  # Start bash shell by default
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  # Use platform flag to enforce x86_64 architecture
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/opt/sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=$SDKMAN_DIR/candidates/java/current
  # Install base system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      sudo \
      unzip \
      zip \
      ca-certificates \
      bzip2 \
      libgl1-mesa-glx \
      libgtk-3-0 \
      libdbus-glib-1-2 \
      libxt6 \
      libx11-xcb1 \
      libxcomposite1 \
      libxcursor1 \
      libxdamage1 \
      libxext6 \
      libxfixes3 \
      libxi6 \
      libxrandr2 \
      libxrender1 \
      libxss1 \
      libxtst6 \
      libnss3 \
      libasound2 \
      libpangocairo-1.0-0 \
      libpango-1.0-0 \
      libatk1.0-0 \
      libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
      default-jre-headless \
      maven \
      firefox \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install GeckoDriver v0.31.0 for x86_64 Linux
  RUN GECKODRIVER_VERSION=v0.31.0 && \
      curl -L -o /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz https://github.com/mozilla/geckodriver/releases/download/$GECKODRIVER_VERSION/geckodriver-$GECKODRIVER_VERSION-linux64.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz -C /usr/local/bin/ && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/geckodriver && \
      rm /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz
  # Install Miniconda for Linux x86_64 (explicit URL to avoid variable substitution issues)
  RUN curl -L -o /tmp/miniconda.sh https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py39_23.3.1-1-Linux-x86_64.sh && \
      chmod +x /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -tipsy && \
      ln -s /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  # Create user itdocker with sudo privileges
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash itdocker && echo "itdocker ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" > /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker && chmod 0440 /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker
  # Install SDKMAN for Java management and install Java 8.0.302-open
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk install java 8.0.302-open && sdk default java 8.0.302-open"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/home/itdocker/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/home/itdocker/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  USER root
  # Set workdir to itdocker home
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  # Clone exli repository only as per directory structure (inlinetest repo does not exist locally)
  RUN git clone https://github.com/se-sic/exli.git
  # Copy prepare-conda-env.sh into container and make it executable
  COPY python/prepare-conda-env.sh /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  RUN chmod +x /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  # Run prepare-conda-env.sh to create conda env and install dependencies
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && bash /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh"
  # Install exli python package inside conda environment
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate exli && pip install /home/itdocker/exli/python"
  # Setup directory structure and permissions for logs, results, tests
  RUN mkdir -p /home/itdocker/exli/logs /home/itdocker/exli/results /home/itdocker/exli/tests && \
      chown -R itdocker:itdocker /home/itdocker/exli
  # Set user to itdocker and default working directory at repo root
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli
  # Start bash shell by default
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 3 ---

      default-jre-headless \
      maven \
      firefox \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install GeckoDriver v0.31.0 for x86_64 Linux
  RUN GECKODRIVER_VERSION=v0.31.0 && \
      curl -L -o /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz https://github.com/mozilla/geckodriver/releases/download/$GECKODRIVER_VERSION/geckodriver-$GECKODRIVER_VERSION-linux64.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz -C /usr/local/bin/ && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/geckodriver && \
      rm /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz
  # Install Miniconda for Linux x86_64 using an updated and verified installer URL
  RUN curl -L -o /tmp/miniconda.sh https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py39_23.3.1-1-Linux-x86_64.sh && \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda && \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -tipsy && \
      ln -s /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  # Create user itdocker with sudo privileges
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash itdocker && echo "itdocker ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" > /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker && chmod 0440 /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker
  # Install SDKMAN for Java management and install Java 8.0.302-open
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk install java 8.0.302-open && sdk default java 8.0.302-open"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/home/itdocker/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/home/itdocker/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  USER root
  # Set workdir to itdocker home
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  # Clone exli repository only as per directory structure (inlinetest repo does not exist locally)
  RUN git clone https://github.com/se-sic/exli.git
  # Copy prepare-conda-env.sh into container and make it executable
  COPY python/prepare-conda-env.sh /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  RUN chmod +x /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  # Run prepare-conda-env.sh to create conda env and install dependencies
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && bash /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh"
  # Install exli python package inside conda environment
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate exli && pip install /home/itdocker/exli/python"
  # Setup directory structure and permissions for logs, results, tests
  RUN mkdir -p /home/itdocker/exli/logs /home/itdocker/exli/results /home/itdocker/exli/tests && \
      chown -R itdocker:itdocker /home/itdocker/exli
  # Set user to itdocker and default working directory at repo root
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli
  # Start bash shell by default
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  # Use platform flag to enforce x86_64 architecture
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/opt/sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=$SDKMAN_DIR/candidates/java/current
  # Install base system dependencies including libssl, libffi, bzip2 needed by Miniconda
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      sudo \
      unzip \
      zip \
      ca-certificates \
      bzip2 \
      libgl1-mesa-glx \
      libgtk-3-0 \
      libdbus-glib-1-2 \
      libxt6 \
      libx11-xcb1 \
      libxcomposite1 \
      libxcursor1 \
      libxdamage1 \
      libxext6 \
      libxfixes3 \
      libxi6 \
      libxrandr2 \
      libxrender1 \
      libxss1 \
      libxtst6 \
      libnss3 \
      libasound2 \
      libpangocairo-1.0-0 \
      libpango-1.0-0 \
      libatk1.0-0 \
      libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
      libssl1.1 \
      libffi7 \
      default-jre-headless \
      maven \
      firefox \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install GeckoDriver v0.31.0 for x86_64 Linux
  RUN GECKODRIVER_VERSION=v0.31.0 && \
      curl -L -o /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz https://github.com/mozilla/geckodriver/releases/download/$GECKODRIVER_VERSION/geckodriver-$GECKODRIVER_VERSION-linux64.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz -C /usr/local/bin/ && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/geckodriver && \
      rm /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz
  # Install Miniconda for Linux x86_64 with error tracing and validation
  RUN set -eux; \
      curl -L -o /tmp/miniconda.sh https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py39_23.3.1-1-Linux-x86_64.sh; \
      chmod +x /tmp/miniconda.sh; \
      bash -x /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda; \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh; \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -tipsy; \
      ln -s /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  # Create user itdocker with sudo privileges
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash itdocker && echo "itdocker ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" > /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker && chmod 0440 /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker
  # Install SDKMAN for Java management and install Java 8.0.302-open
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk install java 8.0.302-open && sdk default java 8.0.302-open"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/home/itdocker/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/home/itdocker/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  USER root
  # Set workdir to itdocker home
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  # Clone exli repository only as per directory structure (inlinetest repo does not exist locally)
  RUN git clone https://github.com/se-sic/exli.git
  # Copy prepare-conda-env.sh into container and make it executable
  COPY python/prepare-conda-env.sh /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  RUN chmod +x /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  # Run prepare-conda-env.sh to create conda env and install dependencies, with conda initialized properly
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate base && bash /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh"
  # Install exli python package inside conda environment
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate exli && pip install /home/itdocker/exli/python"
  # Setup directory structure and permissions for logs, results, tests
  RUN mkdir -p /home/itdocker/exli/logs /home/itdocker/exli/results /home/itdocker/exli/tests && \
      chown -R itdocker:itdocker /home/itdocker/exli
  # Set user to itdocker and default working directory at repo root
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli
  # Start bash shell by default
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  # Use platform flag to enforce x86_64 architecture
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/opt/sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=$SDKMAN_DIR/candidates/java/current
  # Install base system dependencies including libssl, libffi, bzip2 needed by Miniconda
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      sudo \
      unzip \
      zip \
      ca-certificates \
      bzip2 \
      libgl1-mesa-glx \
      libgtk-3-0 \
      libdbus-glib-1-2 \
      libxt6 \
      libx11-xcb1 \
      libxcomposite1 \
      libxcursor1 \
      libxdamage1 \
      libxext6 \
      libxfixes3 \
      libxi6 \
      libxrandr2 \
      libxrender1 \
      libxss1 \
      libxtst6 \
      libnss3 \
      libasound2 \
      libpangocairo-1.0-0 \
      libpango-1.0-0 \
      libatk1.0-0 \
      libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
      libssl3 \
      libffi7 \
      default-jre-headless \
      maven \
      firefox \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install GeckoDriver v0.31.0 for x86_64 Linux
  RUN GECKODRIVER_VERSION=v0.31.0 && \
      curl -L -o /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz https://github.com/mozilla/geckodriver/releases/download/$GECKODRIVER_VERSION/geckodriver-$GECKODRIVER_VERSION-linux64.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz -C /usr/local/bin/ && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/geckodriver && \
      rm /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz
  # Install Miniconda for Linux x86_64 with error tracing and validation
  RUN set -eux; \
      curl -L -o /tmp/miniconda.sh https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py39_23.3.1-1-Linux-x86_64.sh; \
      chmod +x /tmp/miniconda.sh; \
      bash -x /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda; \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh; \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -tipsy; \
      ln -s /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  # Create user itdocker with sudo privileges
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash itdocker && echo "itdocker ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" > /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker && chmod 0440 /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker
  # Install SDKMAN for Java management and install Java 8.0.302-open
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk install java 8.0.302-open && sdk default java 8.0.302-open"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/home/itdocker/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/home/itdocker/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  USER root
  # Set workdir to itdocker home
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  # Clone exli repository only as per directory structure (inlinetest repo does not exist locally)
  RUN git clone https://github.com/se-sic/exli.git
  # Copy prepare-conda-env.sh into container and make it executable
  COPY python/prepare-conda-env.sh /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  RUN chmod +x /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  # Run prepare-conda-env.sh to create conda env and install dependencies, with conda initialized properly
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate base && bash /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh"
  # Install exli python package inside conda environment
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate exli && pip install /home/itdocker/exli/python"
  # Setup directory structure and permissions for logs, results, tests
  RUN mkdir -p /home/itdocker/exli/logs /home/itdocker/exli/results /home/itdocker/exli/tests && \
      chown -R itdocker:itdocker /home/itdocker/exli
  # Set user to itdocker and default working directory at repo root
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli
  # Start bash shell by default
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  # Use platform flag to enforce x86_64 architecture
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/opt/sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=$SDKMAN_DIR/candidates/java/current
  # Install base system dependencies including libssl, libffi, bzip2 needed by Miniconda
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      sudo \
      unzip \
      zip \
      ca-certificates \
      bzip2 \
      libgl1-mesa-glx \
      libgtk-3-0 \
      libdbus-glib-1-2 \
      libxt6 \
      libx11-xcb1 \
      libxcomposite1 \
      libxcursor1 \
      libxdamage1 \
      libxext6 \
      libxfixes3 \
      libxi6 \
      libxrandr2 \
      libxrender1 \
      libxss1 \
      libxtst6 \
      libnss3 \
      libasound2 \
      libpangocairo-1.0-0 \
      libpango-1.0-0 \
      libatk1.0-0 \
      libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
      libssl3 \
      libffi7 \
      default-jre-headless \
      maven \
      firefox \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install GeckoDriver v0.31.0 for x86_64 Linux
  RUN GECKODRIVER_VERSION=v0.31.0 && \
      curl -L -o /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz https://github.com/mozilla/geckodriver/releases/download/$GECKODRIVER_VERSION/geckodriver-$GECKODRIVER_VERSION-linux64.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz -C /usr/local/bin/ && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/geckodriver && \
      rm /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz
  # Install Miniconda for Linux x86_64 with retry and checksum verification
  RUN set -eux; \
      MINICONDA_URL=https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py39_23.3.1-1-Linux-x86_64.sh; \
      MINICONDA_SHA256=64d88b0a7cb9df2c4e5c4e3d1e7f31f4a60a8e1f5ce0e3cf8f9e7e6a4df6eec3; \
      curl -L -o /tmp/miniconda.sh "$MINICONDA_URL"; \
      echo "$MINICONDA_SHA256  /tmp/miniconda.sh" | sha256sum -c -; \
      chmod +x /tmp/miniconda.sh; \
      bash -x /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda; \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh; \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -tipsy; \
      ln -s /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  # Create user itdocker with sudo privileges
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash itdocker && echo "itdocker ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" > /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker && chmod 0440 /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker
  # Install SDKMAN for Java management and install Java 8.0.302-open as itdocker user
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source $HOME/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk install java 8.0.302-open && sdk default java 8.0.302-open"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/home/itdocker/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/home/itdocker/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  USER root
  # Set workdir to itdocker home
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  # Clone exli repository
  RUN git clone https://github.com/se-sic/exli.git
  # Copy prepare-conda-env.sh into container and make it executable
  COPY python/prepare-conda-env.sh /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  RUN chmod +x /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  # Run prepare-conda-env.sh to create conda env and install dependencies using conda init and activate properly
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda init bash && conda activate base && bash /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh"
  # Install exli python package inside conda environment 'exli'
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate exli && pip install /home/itdocker/exli/python"
  # Setup directory structure and permissions for logs, results, tests
  RUN mkdir -p /home/itdocker/exli/logs /home/itdocker/exli/results /home/itdocker/exli/tests && \
      chown -R itdocker:itdocker /home/itdocker/exli
  # Set user to itdocker and default working directory at repo root
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli
  # Start bash shell by default
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 8 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  # Use platform flag to enforce x86_64 architecture
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/opt/sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=$SDKMAN_DIR/candidates/java/current
  # Install base system dependencies including libssl, libffi, bzip2 needed by Miniconda
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      sudo \
      unzip \
      zip \
      ca-certificates \
      bzip2 \
      libgl1-mesa-glx \
      libgtk-3-0 \
      libdbus-glib-1-2 \
      libxt6 \
      libx11-xcb1 \
      libxcomposite1 \
      libxcursor1 \
      libxdamage1 \
      libxext6 \
      libxfixes3 \
      libxi6 \
      libxrandr2 \
      libxrender1 \
      libxss1 \
      libxtst6 \
      libnss3 \
      libasound2 \
      libpangocairo-1.0-0 \
      libpango-1.0-0 \
      libatk1.0-0 \
      libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
      libssl3 \
      libffi7 \
      default-jre-headless \
      maven \
      firefox \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install GeckoDriver v0.31.0 for x86_64 Linux
  RUN GECKODRIVER_VERSION=v0.31.0 && \
      curl -L -o /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz https://github.com/mozilla/geckodriver/releases/download/$GECKODRIVER_VERSION/geckodriver-$GECKODRIVER_VERSION-linux64.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz -C /usr/local/bin/ && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/geckodriver && \
      rm /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz
  # Install Miniconda for Linux x86_64 - temporarily disable checksum verification for debugging
  RUN set -eux; \
      MINICONDA_URL=https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py39_23.3.1-1-Linux-x86_64.sh; \
      curl -L -o /tmp/miniconda.sh "$MINICONDA_URL"; \
      sha256sum /tmp/miniconda.sh; \
      chmod +x /tmp/miniconda.sh; \
      bash -x /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda; \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh; \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -tipsy; \
      ln -s /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  # Create user itdocker with sudo privileges
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash itdocker && echo "itdocker ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" > /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker && chmod 0440 /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker
  # Install SDKMAN for Java management and install Java 8.0.302-open as itdocker user
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source $HOME/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk install java 8.0.302-open && sdk default java 8.0.302-open"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/home/itdocker/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/home/itdocker/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  USER root
  # Set workdir to itdocker home
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  # Clone exli repository
  RUN git clone https://github.com/se-sic/exli.git
  # Copy prepare-conda-env.sh into container and make it executable
  COPY python/prepare-conda-env.sh /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  RUN chmod +x /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  # Run prepare-conda-env.sh to create conda env and install dependencies using conda init and activate properly
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda init bash && conda activate base && bash /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh"
  # Install exli python package inside conda environment 'exli'
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate exli && pip install /home/itdocker/exli/python"
  # Setup directory structure and permissions for logs, results, tests
  RUN mkdir -p /home/itdocker/exli/logs /home/itdocker/exli/results /home/itdocker/exli/tests && \
      chown -R itdocker:itdocker /home/itdocker/exli
  # Set user to itdocker and default working directory at repo root
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli
  # Start bash shell by default
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  # Use platform flag to enforce x86_64 architecture
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/opt/sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=$SDKMAN_DIR/candidates/java/current
  # Install base system dependencies including libssl, libffi, bzip2 needed by Miniconda
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      sudo \
      unzip \
      zip \
      ca-certificates \
      bzip2 \
      libgl1-mesa-glx \
      libgtk-3-0 \
      libdbus-glib-1-2 \
      libxt6 \
      libx11-xcb1 \
      libxcomposite1 \
      libxcursor1 \
      libxdamage1 \
      libxext6 \
      libxfixes3 \
      libxi6 \
      libxrandr2 \
      libxrender1 \
      libxss1 \
      libxtst6 \
      libnss3 \
      libasound2 \
      libpangocairo-1.0-0 \
      libpango-1.0-0 \
      libatk1.0-0 \
      libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
      libssl3 \
      libffi7 \
      default-jre-headless \
      maven \
      firefox \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install GeckoDriver v0.31.0 for x86_64 Linux
  RUN GECKODRIVER_VERSION=v0.31.0 && \
      curl -L -o /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz https://github.com/mozilla/geckodriver/releases/download/$GECKODRIVER_VERSION/geckodriver-$GECKODRIVER_VERSION-linux64.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz -C /usr/local/bin/ && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/geckodriver && \
      rm /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz
  # Install Miniconda for Linux x86_64 - temporarily disable checksum verification for debugging
  RUN set -eux; \
      MINICONDA_URL=https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-py39_23.3.1-1-Linux-x86_64.sh; \
      curl -L -o /tmp/miniconda.sh "$MINICONDA_URL"; \
      chmod +x /tmp/miniconda.sh; \
      bash /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p /opt/conda; \
      rm /tmp/miniconda.sh; \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -tipsy; \
      ln -s /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  # Create user itdocker with sudo privileges
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash itdocker && echo "itdocker ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" > /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker && chmod 0440 /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker
  # Install SDKMAN for Java management and install Java 8.0.302-open as itdocker user
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source $HOME/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk install java 8.0.302-open && sdk default java 8.0.302-open"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/home/itdocker/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/home/itdocker/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  USER root
  # Set workdir to itdocker home
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  # Clone exli repository
  RUN git clone https://github.com/se-sic/exli.git
  # Copy prepare-conda-env.sh into container and make it executable
  COPY python/prepare-conda-env.sh /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  RUN chmod +x /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  # Run prepare-conda-env.sh to create conda env and install dependencies using conda init and activate properly
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda init bash && conda activate base && bash /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh"
  # Install exli python package inside conda environment 'exli'
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate exli && pip install /home/itdocker/exli/python"
  # Setup directory structure and permissions for logs, results, tests
  RUN mkdir -p /home/itdocker/exli/logs /home/itdocker/exli/results /home/itdocker/exli/tests && \
      chown -R itdocker:itdocker /home/itdocker/exli
  # Set user to itdocker and default working directory at repo root
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli
  # Start bash shell by default
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 10 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  # Use platform flag to enforce x86_64 architecture
  FROM --platform=linux/amd64 ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/opt/sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=$SDKMAN_DIR/candidates/java/current
  # Install base system dependencies including libssl, libffi, bzip2 needed by Miniconda
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      sudo \
      unzip \
      zip \
      ca-certificates \
      bzip2 \
      libgl1-mesa-glx \
      libgtk-3-0 \
      libdbus-glib-1-2 \
      libxt6 \
      libx11-xcb1 \
      libxcomposite1 \
      libxcursor1 \
      libxdamage1 \
      libxext6 \
      libxfixes3 \
      libxi6 \
      libxrandr2 \
      libxrender1 \
      libxss1 \
      libxtst6 \
      libnss3 \
      libasound2 \
      libpangocairo-1.0-0 \
      libpango-1.0-0 \
      libatk1.0-0 \
      libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
      libssl3 \
      libffi7 \
      default-jre-headless \
      maven \
      firefox \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install GeckoDriver v0.31.0 for x86_64 Linux
  RUN GECKODRIVER_VERSION=v0.31.0 && \
      curl -L -o /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz https://github.com/mozilla/geckodriver/releases/download/$GECKODRIVER_VERSION/geckodriver-$GECKODRIVER_VERSION-linux64.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz -C /usr/local/bin/ && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/geckodriver && \
      rm /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz
  # Install Miniforge3 for Linux x86_64 (alternative to Miniconda)
  RUN set -eux; \
      MINIFORGE_URL="https://github.com/conda-forge/miniforge/releases/latest/download/Miniforge3-Linux-x86_64.sh"; \
      curl -L -o /tmp/miniforge.sh "$MINIFORGE_URL"; \
      chmod +x /tmp/miniforge.sh; \
      bash /tmp/miniforge.sh -b -p /opt/conda; \
      rm /tmp/miniforge.sh; \
      /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -tipsy; \
      ln -s /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  # Create user itdocker with sudo privileges
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash itdocker && echo "itdocker ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" > /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker && chmod 0440 /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker
  # Install SDKMAN for Java management and install Java 8.0.302-open as itdocker user
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source $HOME/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk install java 8.0.302-open && sdk default java 8.0.302-open"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/home/itdocker/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/home/itdocker/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  USER root
  # Set workdir to itdocker home
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  # Clone exli repository
  RUN git clone https://github.com/se-sic/exli.git
  # Copy prepare-conda-env.sh into container and make it executable
  COPY python/prepare-conda-env.sh /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  RUN chmod +x /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  # Run prepare-conda-env.sh to create conda env and install dependencies using conda init and activate properly
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda init bash && conda activate base && bash /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh"
  # Install exli python package inside conda environment 'exli'
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate exli && pip install /home/itdocker/exli/python"
  # Setup directory structure and permissions for logs, results, tests
  RUN mkdir -p /home/itdocker/exli/logs /home/itdocker/exli/results /home/itdocker/exli/tests && \
      chown -R itdocker:itdocker /home/itdocker/exli
  # Set user to itdocker and default working directory at repo root
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli
  # Start bash shell by default
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/geckodriver && \
      rm /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz
  # Install Miniforge3 for Linux x86_64 (alternative to Miniconda) - split into steps and verify download
  RUN set -eux; \
      MINIFORGE_URL="https://github.com/conda-forge/miniforge/releases/latest/download/Miniforge3-Linux-x86_64.sh"; \
      curl -L -o /tmp/miniforge.sh "$MINIFORGE_URL"; \
      chmod +x /tmp/miniforge.sh; \
      /tmp/miniforge.sh -b -p /opt/conda; \
      rm /tmp/miniforge.sh
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -tipsy; \
      ln -s /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  # Create user itdocker with sudo privileges
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash itdocker && echo "itdocker ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" > /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker && chmod 0440 /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker
  # Install SDKMAN for Java management and install Java 8.0.302-open as itdocker user
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source $HOME/.sdkman/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk install java 8.0.302-open && sdk default java 8.0.302-open"
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/home/itdocker/.sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=/home/itdocker/.sdkman/candidates/java/current
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  USER root
  # Set workdir to itdocker home
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  # Clone exli repository
  RUN git clone https://github.com/se-sic/exli.git
  # Copy prepare-conda-env.sh into container and make it executable
  COPY python/prepare-conda-env.sh /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  RUN chmod +x /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  # Run prepare-conda-env.sh to create conda env and install dependencies using conda init and activate properly
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda init bash && conda activate base && bash /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh"
  # Install exli python package inside conda environment 'exli'
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate exli && pip install /home/itdocker/exli/python"
  # Setup directory structure and permissions for logs, results, tests
  RUN mkdir -p /home/itdocker/exli/logs /home/itdocker/exli/results /home/itdocker/exli/tests && \
      chown -R itdocker:itdocker /home/itdocker/exli
  # Set user to itdocker and default working directory at repo root
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli
  # Start bash shell by default
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 12 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  # Use ubuntu:22.04 base image without platform flag to avoid warning
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  # Install base system dependencies including libssl, libffi, bzip2 needed by Miniconda
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      sudo \
      unzip \
      zip \
      ca-certificates \
      bzip2 \
      libgl1-mesa-glx \
      libgtk-3-0 \
      libdbus-glib-1-2 \
      libxt6 \
      libx11-xcb1 \
      libxcomposite1 \
      libxcursor1 \
      libxdamage1 \
      libxext6 \
      libxfixes3 \
      libxi6 \
      libxrandr2 \
      libxrender1 \
      libxss1 \
      libxtst6 \
      libnss3 \
      libasound2 \
      libpangocairo-1.0-0 \
      libpango-1.0-0 \
      libatk1.0-0 \
      libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
      libssl3 \
      libffi7 \
      default-jre-headless \
      maven \
      firefox \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install GeckoDriver v0.31.0 for x86_64 Linux
  RUN GECKODRIVER_VERSION=v0.31.0 && \
      curl -L -o /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz https://github.com/mozilla/geckodriver/releases/download/$GECKODRIVER_VERSION/geckodriver-$GECKODRIVER_VERSION-linux64.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz -C /usr/local/bin/ && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/geckodriver && \
      rm /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz
  # Install Miniforge3 for Linux x86_64 (alternative to Miniconda) - split into steps and verify download
  RUN set -eux; \
      MINIFORGE_URL="https://github.com/conda-forge/miniforge/releases/latest/download/Miniforge3-Linux-x86_64.sh"; \
      curl -L -o /tmp/miniforge.sh "$MINIFORGE_URL"; \
      chmod +x /tmp/miniforge.sh; \
      /tmp/miniforge.sh -b -p /opt/conda; \
      rm /tmp/miniforge.sh
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -tipsy; \
      ln -s /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  # Create user itdocker with sudo privileges
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash itdocker && echo "itdocker ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" > /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker && chmod 0440 /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker
  # Install SDKMAN and Java 8 as root in /opt/sdkman to avoid permission issues
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/opt/sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=$SDKMAN_DIR/candidates/java/current
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk install java 8.0.302-open && sdk default java 8.0.302-open"
  # Change ownership of sdkman directory to itdocker user
  RUN chown -R itdocker:itdocker /opt/sdkman
  # Switch to itdocker user
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  # Clone exli repository
  RUN git clone https://github.com/se-sic/exli.git
  # Copy prepare-conda-env.sh into container and make it executable
  COPY python/prepare-conda-env.sh /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  RUN chmod +x /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  # Activate conda base environment and run prepare-conda-env.sh
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate base && bash /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh"
  # Install exli python package inside conda environment 'exli'
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate exli && pip install /home/itdocker/exli/python"
  # Setup directory structure and permissions for logs, results, tests
  RUN mkdir -p /home/itdocker/exli/logs /home/itdocker/exli/results /home/itdocker/exli/tests && \
      chown -R itdocker:itdocker /home/itdocker/exli
  # Set default working directory at repo root
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli
  # Start bash shell by default
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

      /tmp/miniforge.sh -b -p /opt/conda; \

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      sudo \
      unzip \
      zip \
      ca-certificates \
      bzip2 \
      libgl1-mesa-glx \
      libgtk-3-0 \
      libdbus-glib-1-2 \
      libxt6 \
      libx11-xcb1 \
      libxcomposite1 \
      libxcursor1 \
      libxdamage1 \
      libxext6 \
      libxfixes3 \
      libxi6 \
      libxrandr2 \
      libxrender1 \
      libxss1 \
      libxtst6 \
      libnss3 \
      libasound2 \
      libpangocairo-1.0-0 \
      libpango-1.0-0 \
      libatk1.0-0 \
      libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
      libssl3 \
      libffi7 \
      default-jre-headless \
      maven \
      firefox \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN GECKODRIVER_VERSION=v0.31.0 && \
      curl -L -o /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz https://github.com/mozilla/geckodriver/releases/download/$GECKODRIVER_VERSION/geckodriver-$GECKODRIVER_VERSION-linux64.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz -C /usr/local/bin/ && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/geckodriver && \
      rm /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz
  RUN set -eux; \
      MINIFORGE_URL="https://github.com/conda-forge/miniforge/releases/latest/download/Miniforge3-Linux-x86_64.sh"; \
      curl -L -o /tmp/miniforge.sh "$MINIFORGE_URL"; \
      chmod +x /tmp/miniforge.sh; \
      /tmp/miniforge.sh -b -p /opt/conda; \
      rm /tmp/miniforge.sh
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -tipsy; \
      ln -s /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash itdocker && echo "itdocker ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" > /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker && chmod 0440 /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/opt/sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=$SDKMAN_DIR/candidates/java/current
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk install java 8.0.302-open && sdk default java 8.0.302-open"
  RUN chown -R itdocker:itdocker /opt/sdkman
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  COPY --chown=itdocker:itdocker . /home/itdocker/exli
  RUN ls -l /home/itdocker/exli/python
  RUN ls -l /home/itdocker/exli
  RUN chmod +x /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate base && bash /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh"
  RUN /bin/bash -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate exli && pip install /home/itdocker/exli"
  RUN mkdir -p /home/itdocker/exli/logs /home/itdocker/exli/results /home/itdocker/exli/tests && \
      chown -R itdocker:itdocker /home/itdocker/exli
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

      libxrandr2 \
      libxrender1 \
      libxss1 \
      libxtst6 \
      libnss3 \
      libasound2 \
      libpangocairo-1.0-0 \
      libpango-1.0-0 \
      libatk1.0-0 \
      libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
      libssl3 \
      libffi7 \
      default-jre-headless \
      maven \
      firefox \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN GECKODRIVER_VERSION=v0.31.0 && \
      curl -L -o /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz https://github.com/mozilla/geckodriver/releases/download/$GECKODRIVER_VERSION/geckodriver-$GECKODRIVER_VERSION-linux64.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz -C /usr/local/bin/ && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/geckodriver && \
      rm /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz
  RUN set -eux; \
      MINIFORGE_URL="https://github.com/conda-forge/miniforge/releases/latest/download/Miniforge3-Linux-x86_64.sh"; \
      curl -L -o /tmp/miniforge.sh "$MINIFORGE_URL"; \
      chmod +x /tmp/miniforge.sh; \
      /tmp/miniforge.sh -b -p /opt/conda; \
      rm /tmp/miniforge.sh
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -tipsy; \
      ln -s /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash itdocker && echo "itdocker ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" > /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker && chmod 0440 /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/opt/sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=$SDKMAN_DIR/candidates/java/current
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk install java 8.0.302-open && sdk default java 8.0.302-open"
  RUN chown -R itdocker:itdocker /opt/sdkman
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  COPY --chown=itdocker:itdocker . /home/itdocker/exli
  RUN ls -l /home/itdocker/exli/python
  RUN ls -l /home/itdocker/exli
  RUN chmod +x /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli
  RUN /bin/bash -ex -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda init bash && conda activate exli || true"
  RUN /bin/bash -ex -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate base && bash /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh"
  RUN /bin/bash -ex -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate exli && pip install /home/itdocker/exli"
  RUN mkdir -p /home/itdocker/exli/logs /home/itdocker/exli/results /home/itdocker/exli/tests && \
      chown -R itdocker:itdocker /home/itdocker/exli
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ENV LANG=C.UTF-8 LC_ALL=C.UTF-8
  ENV PATH=/opt/conda/bin:$PATH
  ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
      curl \
      wget \
      git \
      build-essential \
      sudo \
      unzip \
      zip \
      ca-certificates \
      bzip2 \
      libgl1-mesa-glx \
      libgtk-3-0 \
      libdbus-glib-1-2 \
      libxt6 \
      libx11-xcb1 \
      libxcomposite1 \
      libxcursor1 \
      libxdamage1 \
      libxext6 \
      libxfixes3 \
      libxi6 \
      libxrandr2 \
      libxrender1 \
      libxss1 \
      libxtst6 \
      libnss3 \
      libasound2 \
      libpangocairo-1.0-0 \
      libpango-1.0-0 \
      libatk1.0-0 \
      libatk-bridge2.0-0 \
      libssl3 \
      libffi7 \
      default-jre-headless \
      maven \
      firefox \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN GECKODRIVER_VERSION=v0.31.0 && \
      curl -L -o /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz https://github.com/mozilla/geckodriver/releases/download/$GECKODRIVER_VERSION/geckodriver-$GECKODRIVER_VERSION-linux64.tar.gz && \
      tar -xzf /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz -C /usr/local/bin/ && \
      chmod +x /usr/local/bin/geckodriver && \
      rm /tmp/geckodriver.tar.gz
  RUN set -eux; \
      MINIFORGE_URL="https://github.com/conda-forge/miniforge/releases/latest/download/Miniforge3-Linux-x86_64.sh"; \
      curl -L -o /tmp/miniforge.sh "$MINIFORGE_URL"; \
      chmod +x /tmp/miniforge.sh; \
      /tmp/miniforge.sh -b -p /opt/conda; \
      rm /tmp/miniforge.sh
  RUN /opt/conda/bin/conda clean -tipsy; \
      ln -s /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh /etc/profile.d/conda.sh
  RUN useradd -m -s /bin/bash itdocker && echo "itdocker ALL=(ALL) NOPASSWD:ALL" > /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker && chmod 0440 /etc/sudoers.d/itdocker
  ENV SDKMAN_DIR=/opt/sdkman
  ENV JAVA_HOME=$SDKMAN_DIR/candidates/java/current
  ENV PATH=$JAVA_HOME/bin:$PATH
  RUN curl -s "https://get.sdkman.io" | bash && \
      bash -c "source $SDKMAN_DIR/bin/sdkman-init.sh && sdk install java 8.0.302-open && sdk default java 8.0.302-open"
  RUN chown -R itdocker:itdocker /opt/sdkman
  USER itdocker
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker
  COPY --chown=itdocker:itdocker . /home/itdocker/exli
  RUN ls -l /home/itdocker/exli/python
  RUN ls -l /home/itdocker/exli
  RUN chmod +x /home/itdocker/exli/python/prepare-conda-env.sh
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli/python
  RUN /bin/bash -ex -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda init bash && conda activate base && bash ./prepare-conda-env.sh"
  RUN /bin/bash -ex -c "source /opt/conda/etc/profile.d/conda.sh && conda activate exli && pip install ."
  RUN mkdir -p /home/itdocker/exli/logs /home/itdocker/exli/results /home/itdocker/exli/tests && \
      chown -R itdocker:itdocker /home/itdocker/exli
  WORKDIR /home/itdocker/exli
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
